localrule call_somatic_sv_delly:
    input: analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.bam, analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.bam.bai, analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_BL.bam, analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_BL.bam.bai, /mnt/backedup/home/jiaZ/working/data/genome/reference.fasta
    output: analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.pre.bcf, analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.tsv, analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.vcf
    jobid: 212
    reason: Missing output files: analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.vcf; Input files updated by another job: analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_BL.bam.bai, analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.bam.bai, analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.bam, analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_BL.bam
    wildcards: flowcell=R10, mode=sup, sample_t=HCC1937_10, sample_n=HCC1937_BL
    threads: 2
    resources: tmpdir=<TBD>, mem=48, walltime=48


        export OMP_NUM_THREADS=2 # delly primarily parallises on the sample level.
        /mnt/backedup/home/jiaZ/working/local/delly/delly lr             -t ALL             -y ont             -o analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.pre.bcf              -g /mnt/backedup/home/jiaZ/working/data/genome/reference.fasta analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.bam analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_BL.bam
        
        function get_sample_id() {
            echo "$(samtools view -H ${1} | perl -lne 'print ${1} if /\sSM:(\S+)/' | head -n 1 )"
        }

        TID=$(get_sample_id "analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.bam")
        CID=$(get_sample_id "analysis/bam/R10/sup/HCC1937_BL.bam")
        printf "${TID}\ttumor\n${CID}\tcontrol\n" > analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.tsv

        /mnt/backedup/home/jiaZ/working/local/delly/delly filter             -f somatic             -p             -s analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.tsv             analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.pre.bcf | bcftools view -Ov > analysis/svs/delly/R10/sup/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL/HCC1937_10.HCC1937_BL.vcf
